<li>to <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> jest w rozwiązaniu</li>
</ul>
<p>Jeśli wszystkie <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>b</mi><mi>j</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b_j</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.980548em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> są w <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span></span> i żadnego <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>c</mi><mi>k</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c_k</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.58056em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">k</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> nie ma w <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span></span>, a <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> też nie jest w <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span></span>, to taki model <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span></span> nie jest stabilny.</p>
<p>Każdy atom <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>M</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a \in M</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.5782em; vertical-align: -0.0391em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span></span> (należący do modelu [rozwiązania]) mysi być wyprowadzalny z jakiejś reguły – musi wynikać z jakiejś reguły (wykluczamy błędne koło we wnioskowaniu).</p>
<h2 id="przykłady-3">Przykłady</h2>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>P</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo>←</mo><mi>a</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P_1 = \{ a \leftarrow a.\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.13889em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>– z <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> wynika <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M = \{a\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span> nie jest stabilnym modelem (chociaż <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∅</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M = \emptyset</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.80556em; vertical-align: -0.05556em;"></span><span class="mord">∅</span></span></span></span></span> jest stabilnym modelem) – przykład błędnego koła: nic nie mówi, że <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> musi być.</p>
<hr>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>P</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>b</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P_2 = \{a \leftarrow \neg b. \}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.13889em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>– czytaj: jeśli w odpowiedzi (<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{ a\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span>) nie ma <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span></span></span></span></span>, to <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> należy do odpowiedzi. Zgadza się: w odpowiedzi nie ma <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span></span></span></span></span>, a więc <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{a\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span> jest jedynym stabilnym modelem: każdy podzbiór atomów (pusty, jednoelementowy z samym <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span>, samym <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span></span></span></span></span> i dwuelementowy <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> i <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span></span></span></span></span>).</p>
<hr>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>P</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>a</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P_3 = \{a \leftarrow \neg a. \}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.13889em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">3</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>– program nie ma stabilnego modelu, skoro jest tylko jeden atom <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span>. Możliwe odpowiedzi: <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∅</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{ \emptyset \}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord">∅</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span> lub  <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span>, ale <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∅</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\emptyset</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.80556em; vertical-align: -0.05556em;"></span><span class="mord">∅</span></span></span></span></span> nie wejdzie do modelu, bo nie jest wyprowadzalne, poza tym z reguły <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>P</mi><mn>3</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P_3</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.13889em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">3</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> wynika, że do modelu ma wejść <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span>.  Do modelu też nie wejdzie <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span>, bo warunkiem wejścia <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> do modelu jest brak <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> w modelu – sprzeczność.</p>
<hr>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>P</mi><mn>4</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>b</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi>b</mi><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>a</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P_4 = \{a \leftarrow \neg b. b \leftarrow \neg a. \}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.13889em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">4</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>Program z dwiema regułami. Ma 2 stabilne modele:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{a\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span> – jeśli w odpowiedzi nie ma <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span></span></span></span></span>, to jest <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> – zgadza się: do modelu dodano <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>b</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{b\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span> – jeśli w odpowiedzi nie ma <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span>, to jest w nim <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span></span></span></span></span>.</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>P</mi><mn>5</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>b</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi>b</mi><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>a</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi>a</mi><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>a</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P_5 = \{ a \leftarrow \neg b. b \leftarrow \neg a. a \leftarrow \neg a. \}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.13889em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">5</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>– <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{a\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span> jest jedynym stabilnym modelem<br>
jeśli a w modelu to b nie ma w modelu (ok), a jest wyprowadzlane (ok)</p>
<h2 id="przykłady-w-języku-ansprolog-w-clingo">Przykłady w języku <code>ansprolog</code> (w <code>Clingo</code>)</h2>
<pre><code>lata(X) :- ptak(X), not nielot(X).
kiedy coś lata: gdy jest ptakiem i nie jest nielotem
nielot(X) :- pingwin(X).
kto jest nielotem - pingwin
ptak(X) :- pingwin(X).
a kto jest ptakiem - pingwin
ptak(antek).
</code></pre>
<p>Zapis <code>:-</code> jest odpowiednikiem <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>←</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\leftarrow</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.36687em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<p>Zmienne: <code>X</code></p>
<p>Stałe: <code>antek</code></p>
<p>Konkluzja: <code>antek</code> lata, bo jest stabilnym modelem: jest <code>ptak(antek)</code>, <code>lata(antek)</code></p>
<p>Jeśli zamienimy fakt <code>pingwin(antek)</code>, wtedy stabilny  model zawiera <code>nielot(antek)</code>.</p>
<h2 id="więzy-ograniczenia">Więzy (ograniczenia)</h2>
<p>Więzy (inaczej ograniczenia) to  reguły bez głowy (z pustą głową), np.</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>←</mo><msub><mi>b</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo>…</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>b</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo>…</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><msub><mi>c</mi><mi>n</mi></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\leftarrow b_1, \dots, b_m, \neg c_1, \dots, \neg c_n.</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.36687em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner">…</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner">…</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">n</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>Słownie: nie może być tak, że jest <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>b</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b_1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.84444em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>, jest <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>b</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b_2</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.84444em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> itd., i nie ma <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c_1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.58056em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c_2</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.58056em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> itd.</p>
<p>Więzy służą zabronieniu czegoś, wskazujż, że żaden stabilny model nie może zawierać wszystkich atomów <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>b</mi><mi>j</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b_j</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.980548em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> i jednocześnie nie zawierać żadnego <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>c</mi><mi>k</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c_k</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.58056em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">k</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>To odpowiedniki równań i nierówności w programowaniu całkowitoliczbowym.</p>
<p>Więzy można zastąpić regułami z głową: wystarczy przed strzałką wstawić atom, którego nigdzie indziej nie użyto.</p>
<h1 id="laboratorium-5--6.12.2020">Laboratorium 5 | 6.12.2020</h1>
<h2 id="zadanie-6.">Zadanie 6.</h2>
<p>Ze bioru: <a href="https://gitlab.com/wojtek3dan/zadania-to/-/blob/master/zadania.md">https://gitlab.com/wojtek3dan/zadania-to/-/blob/master/zadania.md</a></p>
<p>Rozważmy pewną jednoosobową grę, w której rekwizytami są liczby całkowite ułożone w ciągu. W każdym kroku wybieramy dowolną liczbę oprócz dwóch skrajnych i usuwamy ją z ciągu. Zdobywamy za to tyle punktów ile wynosi suma wybranej do usunięcia liczby i jej dwóch przyległych sąsiadów. Gra kończy się, gdy w ciągu zostają dwie liczby. Naszym celem jest maksymalizacja zdobytych punktów. Oczywiście punkty zdobyte w kolejnych krokach sumują się. Na przykład, dla ciągu 2, 1, 5, 3, 4 możemy uzyskać maksymalnie 31 punktów w następujący sposób: usuwamy 3 (12 pkt) -&gt; 2, 1, 5, 4; usuwamy 1 (8 pkt) -&gt; 2, 5, 4; usuwamy 5 (11 pkt) -&gt; 2, 4. Suma = 12 + 8 + 11 = 31.</p>
<p>Napisz program wyznaczający maksymalną możliwą do uzyskania sumę punktów. Zakładamy, że długość wejściowego ciągu nie przekroczy 200, a każdy jego element będzie zawierał się w przedziale [1, 100]. Limit czasowy = 10 sekund.</p>
<hr>
<h2 id="zadanie-3">Zadanie 3</h2>
<p>Ze zbioru <a href="https://gitlab.com/wojtek3dan/zadania-to/-/blob/master/zadania.md">https://gitlab.com/wojtek3dan/zadania-to/-/blob/master/zadania.md</a></p>
<p>Do oddania do 14.12.2020</p>
<p>Tablica <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> zawiera liczby całkowite z zakresu od 1 do 50000<br>
uporządkowane niemalejąco, tzn. <em>a</em>[0]≤_a_[1]≤⋯≤_a_[<em>n</em> − 1].<br>
Znajdź najmniejszą dodatnią liczbę całkowitą,<br>
której nie da się przedstawić jako sumę elementów wybranych<br>
z tablicy <em>a</em> (żaden element z tej tablicy nie może być<br>
użyty więcej niż raz). Na przykład, jeśli <em>a</em> = [1, 1, 2, 9],<br>
to taką najmniejszą liczbą będzie 5.<br>
Zakładamy, że <em>n</em> może wynosić 105.<br>
Limit czasowy = 10 sekund.</p>
<p>wejście tak samo jak w poprzednim:</p>
<ul>
<li>wpisujemy liczbę liczb</li>
<li>wpisujemy liczby</li>
<li>po ostatniej program wykonuje obliczenia</li>
</ul>
<h1 id="wykład-6--12.12.2020--metoda-generuj-ograniczaj">Wykład 6 | 12.12.2020 | Metoda generuj-ograniczaj</h1>
<h2 id="zmienna-pomocnicza-a">Zmienna pomocnicza <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>a</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a'</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.751892em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.751892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></h2>
<p>W tej metodzie wprowadza się atom pomocniczy <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>a</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a'</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.751892em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.751892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>, dzięki czemu można zaznaczyć w programie, że inny atom <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> może należeć do rozwiązania, ale nie musi:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> musi należeć do rozwiązania, gdy nie ma <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>a</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a'</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.751892em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.751892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>: <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><msup><mi>a</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a \leftarrow \neg a'.</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.751892em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.751892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> nie może należeć do rozwiązania (żeby <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>a</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a'</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.751892em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.751892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> mogło): <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>a</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>a</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a' \leftarrow \neg a.</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.751892em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.751892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul>
<p>Daje nam to 2 stabilne modele</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{a\}, \{a'\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.05189em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mclose">}</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.801892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>– ten drugi reprezentuje odpowiedź, że atomu <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> nie ma w rozwiązaniu.</p>
<p>W tej metodzie dochodzimy do sytuacji, w którym atom jest wybrany lub nie jest wybrany, co można zapisać regułami jak wyżej.</p>
<p>Pozwala to uzyskać tyle stabilnych modeli, ile jest zmiennych, plus model ze zbiorem pustym, np. dla zbioru stałych <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>b</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>c</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{a, b, c\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span> możemy zapisać reguły:</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><msup><mi>a</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mtext>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</mtext><mi>b</mi><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><msup><mi>b</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mtext>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</mtext><mi>c</mi><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><msup><mi>c</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a \leftarrow \neg a'. \ \ \ \ \ \ b \leftarrow \neg b'. \ \ \ \ \ \ c \leftarrow \neg c'.</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.801892em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.801892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.801892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; <span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>a</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>a</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mtext>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</mtext><msup><mi>b</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>b</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mtext>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</mtext><msup><mi>c</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>c</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a' \leftarrow \neg a. \ \ \ \ \ \ b' \leftarrow \neg b. \ \ \ \ \ \ c' \leftarrow \neg c.</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.801892em; <h2 id="zapis-dodatkowych-warunków">Zapis dodatkowych warunków</h2>
<h3 id="dowolny-podzbiór-zbioru-a-b-c-taki-że-a-i-b-nie-występują-jednocześnie">Dowolny podzbiór zbioru <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>b</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>c</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{a, b, c\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span> taki, że <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> i <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span></span></span></span></span> nie występują jednocześnie</h3>
<p>Zapis:</p>
<p><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><msup><mi>a</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mtext>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</mtext><mi>b</mi><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><msup><mi>b</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mtext>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</mtext><mi>c</mi><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><msup><mi>c</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a \leftarrow \neg a'.\ \ \ \ \ \  b \leftarrow \neg b'. \ \ \ \ \ \  c \leftarrow \neg c'.</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.751892em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.751892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.751892em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.751892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.751892em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.751892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span><br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>a</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>a</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mtext>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</mtext><msup><mi>b</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>b</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mtext>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</mtext><msup><mi>c</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>c</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a' \leftarrow \neg a.\ \ \ \ \ \  b' \leftarrow \neg b. \ \ \ \ \ \  c' \leftarrow \neg c.</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.751892em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.751892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.751892em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.751892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.751892em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.751892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span><br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>←</mo><mi>a</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>b</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\leftarrow a, b.</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.36687em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span>$</p>
<h3 id="jeśli-a-to-b">Jeśli <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span>, to <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span></span></span></span></span></h3>
<p>Inaczej, jeśli <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> jest w stabilnym modelu, to <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span></span></span></span></span> też musi być w modelu:</p>
<p><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi><mo>←</mo><mi>a</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b \leftarrow a.</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<h2 id="przykład-1-cykl-hamiltona-w-grafie">Przykład 1: Cykl Hamiltona w grafie</h2>
<p>W grafie nieskierowanym wskazać <strong>cykl Hamiltona</strong> (cykl, w którym każdy wierzchołek odwiedzany jest tylko 1 raz, za wyjątkiem pierwszego wierzchołka).</p>
<p>Rozwiązanie:</p>
<ul>
<li>patrzymy na cykl Hamiltona nie jak na zbiór wierzchołków, tylko zbiór krawędzi: koniec jednej krawędzi musi być początkiem drugiej</li>
<li>krawędź oznaczymy predykatem:</li>
</ul>
<p><code>krawedz(U, V)</code></p>
<ul>
<li>dowolna krawędź może należeć do tego cyklu, co oznaczymy predykatem:</li>
</ul>
<p><code>wybrana(U, V)</code></p>
<ul>
<li>wybranie krawędzi do rozwiązania:</li>
</ul>
<p><code>wybrana(U, V) :- krawedz(U, V), not odrzucona(U, V).</code></p>
<p>– parę wierzchołków <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>U</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">U</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">U</span></span></span></span></span>, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">V</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span></span></span></span></span> można dodać do rozwiązania, jeśli tworzą krawędź, która nie jest odrzucona (<strong>generowanie krawędzi w rozwiązaniu</strong>)</p>
<ul>
<li>odwrotność wybrania – odrzucenie krawędzi (nienależenie do rozwiązania) (<strong>generowanie krawędzi w rozwiązaniu</strong>):</li>
</ul>
<p><code>odrzucona(U, V) :- krawedz(U, V), not wybrana(U, V).</code></p>
<p>– parę wierzchołków można odrzucić, jeśli tworzą krawędź, która nie jest wybrana</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>powyższe reguły generują wszystkie możliwe podzbiory krawędzi</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>zmienne oznaczające wierzchołki: <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>U</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">U</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">U</span></span></span></span></span>, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">V</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span></span></span></span></span></p>
</li>
<li>
<p>krawędzie w cyklu muszą tworzyć ścieżkę, czyli ciąg połączonych wierzchołków, co oznaczymy regułami (<strong>generowanie wierzchołków osiągalnych</strong>)</p>
</li>
</ul>
<pre><code>osiagalny(V) :- wybrana(v0, V).
osiagalny(V) :- osiagalny(U), wybrana(U, V).
</code></pre>
<p>– gdzie <code>v0</code> oznacza wierzchołek początkowy; pierwsza reguła oznacza możliwość przejścia z wierzchołka <code>v0</code> do dowolnego <code>V</code>, a druga, przejście z <code>U</code> do <code>V</code>, co jednocześnie oznacza przejście z <code>v0</code> do dowolnego wierzchołka <code>V</code></p>
<ul>
<li>z każdego jednego wierzchołka można przejść tylko do jednego innego wierzchołka, co możemy wskazać więzem (<strong>ograniczenie 1.</strong>):</li>
</ul>
<pre><code>:- wybrana(U, V), wybrana(W, V), U != W.
:- wybrana(U, V), wybrana(U, W), V != W.
</code></pre>
<p>– nie może być tak, że jakieś 2 krawędzie wybrane do rozwiązania wchodzą do tego samego wierzchołka <code>V</code></p>
<ul>
<li>ograniczenie zapewniające osiągalność każdego wierzchołka (<strong>ograniczenie 2.</strong>):</li>
</ul>
<pre><code>:- wierzcholek(U), not osiagalny(U).
</code></pre>
<p>– nie może być tak, że <code>U</code> jest wierzchołkiem i nie jest osiągalny (nie można do niego dojść z wierzchołka początkowego lub innego osiągalnego wierzchołka) (<strong>ograniczenie 3.</strong>)</p>
<p>Przykładowe fakty:</p>
<pre><code>wierzcholek(v0).
wierzcholek(v1).
wierzcholek(v2).
krawedz(v0, v1).
krawedz(v1, v0).
krawedz(v1, v2).
krawedz(v2, v0).
</code></pre>
<h2 id="przykład-2-kolorowanie-grafu-przy-użyciu-3-kolorów">Przykład 2: Kolorowanie grafu przy użyciu 3 kolorów</h2>
<p>Pytanie: czy 3 kolorami można pokolorować mapę. Każde państwo może być pokolorowane tylko 1 kolorem. Mapa reprezentowana jest przez zbiór państw i ich granicze:</p>
<p>Rozwiązanie:</p>
<ul>
<li>za mapę przyjmujemy zbiór państw i ich granice, np.</li>
</ul>
<pre><code>panstwo(a).
panstwo(b).
</code></pre>
<ul>
<li>państwa sąsiadujące:</li>
</ul>
<pre><code>sasiedzi(a, b).
</code></pre>
<ul>
<li>kolory:</li>
</ul>
<pre><code>paleta(czerwony).
paleta(niebieski).
paleta(zolty).
</code></pre>
<ul>
<li>reguły potrzebne do sprawdzenia kolorowania mapy: każde państwo zostanie pokolorowane tylko 1 kolorem (<strong>generowanie kolorów</strong>)</li>
</ul>
<pre><code>kolor(V,K) :- panstwo(V), paleta(K), not innyKolor(V,K).
</code></pre>
<p>– państwo <code>V</code> może być pokolorowane <code>K</code>, jeśli <code>K</code> jest kolorem (<code>paleta(k)</code>), <code>V</code> jest państwem (<code>panstwo(V)</code>) i nie jest pokolorowane innym kolorem (<code>not innyKolor(V, K)</code></p>
<ul>
<li>każde państwo musi być pokolorowane (<strong>generowanie innych kolorów</strong> i <strong>generowanie pokolorowanych państw</strong>):</li>
</ul>
<pre><code>innyKolor(V, K) :- panstwo(V), paleta(K), not kolor(V, K).
maKolor(V) :- panstwo(V), paleta(K), kolor(V, K).
</code></pre>
<p>– państwo <code>V</code> może być pokolorowane kolorem <code>K</code>, jeśli <code>V</code> jest państwem (<code>panstwo(V)</code>), <code>K</code> jest kolorem (<code>paleta(K)</code>) i państwo <code>V</code> nie jest pokolorowane innym kolorem (<strong>ograniczenie 1.</strong>):</p>
<pre><code>:- panstwo(V), not maKolor(V).
</code></pre>
<p>– wykluczone jest, że <code>V</code> jest państwem i nie ma koloru</p>
<ul>
<li>każde państwo musi mieć tylko 1 kolor (<strong>ograniczenie 2.</strong>):</li>
</ul>
<pre><code>:- panstwo(V), paleta(K1), paleta(K2), kolor(V, K1), kolor(V, K2), K1 != K2.
</code></pre>
<p>– wykluczone jest, że państwo <code>V</code> ma kolor <code>K1</code> i jednocześnie inny kolor <code>K2</code></p>
<ul>
<li>sąsiadujące państwa nie mogą mieć tego samego koloru (<strong>ograniczenie 3.</strong>):</li>
</ul>
<pre><code>:- sasiedzi(V, U), kolor(V, K), kolor(U, K).
</code></pre>
<p>– dwa państwa, które są sąsiadami, nie mogą mieć tego samego koloru <code>K</code></p>
<p>Fakty:</p>
<pre><code>panstwo(a).
panstwo(b).
sasiedzi(a, b).
paleta(czerwony).
paleta(niebieski).
paleta(zolty).
</code></pre>
<h2 id="grounding">Grounding</h2>
<p>Przed wykonaniem zadania wykonuje się tzw. <strong>grounding</strong> – podstawienie pod zmienne wszystkie możliwe stałe.</p>
<h2 id="formalna-definicja-stabilnego-modelu">Formalna definicja stabilnego modelu</h2>
