<p>Niech <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>P</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span></span></span></span></span> będzie zakotwiczonym programem (bez zmiennych), a <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span></span> podzbiorem jego atomów.</p>
<p><mark><strong>Reduktem</strong></mark> programu <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>P</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span></span></span></span></span> ze wzgledu na <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span></span> nazywamy:</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>P</mi><mi>M</mi></msup><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>h</mi><mo>←</mo><msub><mi>b</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo>…</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>b</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mi>h</mi><mo>←</mo><msub><mi>b</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo>…</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>b</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo>…</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><msub><mi>c</mi><mi>n</mi></msub><mo>∈</mo><mi>P</mi><mo>∧</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo>…</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mi>n</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">}</mo><mo>∩</mo><mi>M</mi><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∅</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P^M = \{h \leftarrow b_1, \dots, b_m | h \leftarrow b_1, \dots, b_m, \neg c_1, \dots, \neg c_n \in P \wedge \{ c_1, \dots, c_n \} \cap M = \emptyset \} </annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.891331em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.891331em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">h</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner">…</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">∣</span><span class="mord mathdefault">h</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner">…</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner">…</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">n</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∧</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner">…</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">n</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">}</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∩</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">∅</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>– bierzemy wszystkie reguły i odcinamy reguły zanegowane <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>c</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span></span></span></span></span>, które nie wchodzą do modelu <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span></span> jest stabilnym modelem dla <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>P</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span></span></span></span></span> wtedy i tylko wtedy, gdy <mark><strong>atomowymi konkluzjami reduktu</strong></mark> jest dokladnie zbiór <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p><strong>Atomowe konkuzje reduktu</strong> – głowy reguł, których wszystkie przesłanki zawarte w ciele (predykaty) są spełnione.</p>
<p>Jeśli tak uzyskany podzbiór atomów (atomowych konkluzji reduktur) jest równy <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span></span>, to <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span></span> jest stabilnym modelem.</p>
<h3 id="przyklad-1">Przyklad 1</h3>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>P</mi><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>b</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mtext>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</mtext><mi>b</mi><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>a</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P = \{ a \leftarrow \neg b. \ \ \ \ \ \ b \leftarrow \neg a. \}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>– jeśli nie zostało wybrane <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span></span></span></span></span>, to musi być wybrane <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span>;<br>
– jeśli nie zostało wybrane <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span>, musi być wybrane <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>Sprawdzenie dla modelu <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M = \{ a \}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span>:</p>
<ul>
<li>patrzymy na każdą regułę:</li>
<li>jeśli nie wybrano <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span></span></span></span></span>, to wybrano <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> – zgadza się, w modelu jest <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> i nie ma <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span></span></span></span></span> – głowę reguły <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> wrzucamy do rozwiązania, mamy pierwszą atomową konkluzję reduktu</li>
<li>jeśli nie wybrano <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span>… ale <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> wybrano, więc regułę pomijamy</li>
</ul>
<p>Zatem odpowiedź: <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M = \{a\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span> jest stabilnym modelem, bo <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>P</mi><mi>M</mi></msup><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P^M = \{a \leftarrow .\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.841331em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.841331em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span>, a jego atomowe klonkluzje to dokladnie zbior <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<h3 id="przykład-3">Przykład 3</h3>
<p>Pytanie: dlaczego <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>a</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a \leftarrow \neg a.</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span> nie ma stabilnego modelu?</p>
<p>W regule jest tylko jeden atom, więc rozważać możemy 2 rozwiązania:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M = \{ a \}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∅</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M = \{ \emptyset \}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord">∅</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul>
<p>– Zbior  pusty nie jest stabilnym modelem, bo nie zawiera <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span>, a zgodnie z regułą powinien:</p>
<ul>
<li>analizowane rozwiązanie: <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∅</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M = \{ \emptyset \}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord">∅</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li>atomowe konkluzje reduktu: <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>P</mi><mi>M</mi></msup><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo>←</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P^M = \{ a \leftarrow .\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.841331em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.841331em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">≠</mi><msup><mi>P</mi><mi>M</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M \neq P^M</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel"><span class="mrel"><span class="mord"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.69444em;"><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="rlap"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="inner"><span class="mrel"></span></span><span class="fix"></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.19444em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mrel">=</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.841331em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.841331em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>, więc <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∅</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{ \emptyset \}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord">∅</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span> nie jest rozwiązaniem</li>
</ul>
<p>– Zbiór <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{ a \}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span> nie jest stabilnym, modelem, bo:</p>
<ul>
<li>analizowane rozwiązanie: <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M = \{ a \}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li>redukt: <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∅</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{ \emptyset \}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord">∅</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span>, bo nie ma niezanegowanych reguł wchodzących do modelu (jest tylko zanegowana <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\neg a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span>)</li>
<li>atomowe konkluzje reduktu (głowy reguł): <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>P</mi><mi>M</mi></msup><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∅</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P^M = \{ \emptyset \}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.841331em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.841331em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord">∅</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">≠</mi><msup><mi>P</mi><mi>M</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M \neq P^M</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel"><span class="mrel"><span class="mord"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.69444em;"><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="rlap"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="inner"><span class="mrel"></span></span><span class="fix"></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.19444em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mrel">=</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.841331em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.841331em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>, bo <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">≠</mi><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∅</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{ a \} \neq \{ \emptyset \}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mclose">}</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel"><span class="mrel"><span class="mord"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.69444em;"><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="rlap"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="inner"><span class="mrel"></span></span><span class="fix"></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.19444em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mrel">=</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord">∅</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span>, więc reguła nie ma stabilnego modelu.</li>
</ul>
<h1 id="laboratorium-6--13.12.2020--niestandardowe-konstrukcje-w-clingo">Laboratorium 6 | 13.12.2020 | Niestandardowe konstrukcje w <code>Clingo</code></h1>
<h2 id="określona-liczba-elementów">Określona liczba elementów</h2>
<p>– Nie mniej niż <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>L</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">L</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">L</span></span></span></span></span> i nie więcej niż <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>U</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">U</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">U</span></span></span></span></span>:</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>L</mi><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo separator="true">;</mo><mo>…</mo> <mo separator="true">;</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo separator="true">;</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><msub><mi>b</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo separator="true">;</mo><mo>…</mo> <mo separator="true">;</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><msub><mi>b</mi><mi>k</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">}</mo><mi>U</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">L \{ a_1; \dots; a_m; \neg b_1; \dots; \neg b_k \} U</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">L</span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner">…</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mpunct">;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner">…</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mpunct">;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">k</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">}</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">U</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<h3 id="przykład-1-0--a-b-not-d-2.">Przykład 1: <code>0 { a; b; not d} 2.</code></h3>
<pre><code>0 { a; b; not d} 2.
</code></pre>
<p>– wybieramy zbiory 0-elementowe, 1-elementowe (<code>a</code>, <code>b</code> lub <code>c</code>) lub 2-elementowe.</p>
<p>Ograniczenie może być z lewej, z prawej, albo z obu stron.</p>
<p>Więzy te mogą być użyte w dowolnym miejscu reguły.</p>
<p><code>{a}</code> jest stabilnym modelem</p>
<p><code>{a, b}</code> nie jest stabilnym modelem, bo już <code>{a}</code> oznacza wybranie 2 elementów: wybranie <code>a</code> i niewybranie <code>d</code></p>
<h3 id="przykład-2-generowanie-wszystkich-podzbiorów--a-b-c-d--takich-że-a-rightarrow-b">Przykład 2: generowanie wszystkich podzbiorów <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>b</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>c</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>d</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{ a, b, c, d \}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">d</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span> takich, że <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi><mo>→</mo><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a \rightarrow b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">→</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span></span></span></span></span></h3>
<p>Wygenerować wszystkie podzbiory <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>b</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>c</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>d</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{a, b, c, d\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">d</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span> w taki sposób, by wybranie <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> pociągało za sobą wybranie <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<p>Zapis w <code>Clingo</code>:</p>
<pre class=" language-clingo"><code class="prism  language-clingo">0 {a; b; c; d} 4.
b :- a.
</code></pre>
<h2 id="skrótowy-zapis-4-faktów-p1..4">Skrótowy zapis 4 faktów: <code>p(1..4)</code></h2>
<p><code>p(1..4).</code> to inaczej:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>p(1)</code></li>
<li><code>p(2)</code></li>
<li><code>p(3)</code></li>
<li><code>p(4)</code></li>
</ul>
<h2 id="kolekcje-z-których-wybieramy-n-elementów">Kolekcje, z których wybieramy <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>n</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">n</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">n</span></span></span></span></span> elementów</h2>
<p><code>{q(X, Y) : p(X)} = 2 :- p(Y).</code></p>
<p>– jeśli <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>p</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>X</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>p</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>p</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>2</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>p</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>3</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>p</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>4</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">p(X) = \{ p(1), p(2), p(3), p(4) \}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">p</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">p</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">p</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">p</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">3</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">p</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">4</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span>, to z kolekcji</p>
<ul>
<li><code>q(1, 1)</code></li>
<li><code>q(2, 1)</code></li>
<li><code>q(3, 1)</code></li>
<li><code>q(4, 1)</code></li>
<li><code>q(1, 2)</code></li>
<li><code>q(2, 2)</code></li>
<li><code>q(3, 2)</code></li>
<li><code>q(4, 2)</code></li>
<li><code>q(1, 3)</code></li>
<li><code>q(2, 3)</code></li>
<li><code>q(3, 3)</code></li>
<li><code>q(4, 3)</code></li>
<li><code>q(1, 4)</code></li>
<li><code>q(2, 4)</code></li>
<li><code>q(3, 4)</code></li>
<li><code>q(4, 4)</code></li>
</ul>
<p>wybieramy 2 elementy.</p>
<h3 id="przykład-generowanie-podzbiorów-a-b-c-d-takich-że-pominięcie-a-implikuje-b">Przykład: generowanie podzbiorów <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>b</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>c</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>d</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{a, b, c, d\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">d</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span> takich, że pominięcie <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> implikuje <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span></span></span></span></span></h3>
<p>Wygeneruj wszystkie podzbiory <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>b</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>c</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>d</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{a, b, c, d\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">d</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span>, aby pominięcie <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> implikowało <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span></span></span></span></span>:</p>
<p><code>0 {a; b; c; d}.</code></p>
<p>– podzbiory od 0-elementowych, przez 1-elementowe, 2 itd. aż do 4, bo są tylko 4 elementy</p>
<p><code>b :- not a.</code></p>
<p>– pominięcie <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> implikuje <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<p>Czy to są stabilne modele dla ww. programu?</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>M</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>b</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>c</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M_1 = \{a, b, c\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.10903em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span> – tak: nie ma reguły mówiącej, że wybranie <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> oznacza brak <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span></span></span></span></span>; jest reguła, że jeśli nie ma 4a$, to musi być <code>b</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>M</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>b</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>c</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>d</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>e</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M_2 = \{b, c, d, e\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.10903em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">d</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">e</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span> – nie: w programie nie ma <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>e</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">e</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">e</span></span></span></span></span></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="wzajemne-wykluczanie-predykatów-graf-hamiltona">Wzajemne wykluczanie predykatów (graf Hamiltona)</h2>
<p>W grafie Hamiltona dowolna krawędź może należeć do cyklu, ale jeśli należy, to nie jest odrzucona, a jeśli jest odrzucona, to nie należy do cyklu:</p>
<p><code>wybrana(U, V) :- krawedz(U, V), not odrzucona(U, V).</code><br>
<code>odrzucona(U, V) :- krawedz(U, V), not wybrana(U, V).</code></p>
<p>W <code>Clingo</code> można zapisać to krócej:</p>
<p><code>0 { wybrana(U, V) : krawedz(U, V) }.</code></p>
<p>– po prawej mamy wszystkie możliwe krawędzie <code>krawedz(U, V)</code> które zasilają wybrane krawędzie</p>
<p>– wybieramy od 0 do nieskończonej liczby krawędzi</p>
<h1 id="wykład-7--19.12.2020--answer-set-programming-2----przykłady">Wykład 7 | 19.12.2020 | Answer Set Programming (2) – przykłady</h1>
<h2 id="agregacje-i-optymalizacja">Agregacje i optymalizacja</h2>
<p>Niestandardowe konstrukcje. Umożliwjają umożliwiają otrzymywanie pojedynczej wartości ze zbioru danych.</p>
<p>W <code>Clingo</code> zaimplementowano:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>count</code> (moc zbioru, liczność)</li>
<li><code>sum</code> (suma elementów zbioru)</li>
<li><code>max</code> i <code>min</code> (element maks. i minim.)</li>
<li><code>maximize</code> i <code>mnimize</code> (optymalizacja)</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="przykład-1">Przykład 1</h3>
<pre><code>edge(a, b).
edge(b, c).
edge(c, a).

edge(X, Y) :- edge(Y, X).
vertex(X) :- edge(X, Y).
degreeOf(X, N) :- vertex(X), N = #count{X, Y : edge(X, Y)}.

#show degreeOf/2.
</code></pre>
<p>– jeśli mamy <code>edge(X, Y)</code>, to jednocześnie  <code>edge(Y, X)</code> (a więc graf jest nieskierowany)</p>
<p>– wierzchołek <code>X</code> jest wtedy, gdy jest krawędź <code>(X, Y)</code> (wierzchołek staje się faktem)</p>
<p>– predykat <code>degreeOf</code> określa stopień wierzchołka: wierzcholek <code>X</code> ma stopien <code>N</code> pod warunkiem, że <code>X jest</code>vertex<code>, a</code>N<code>jest równe liczbie takich</code>(X, Y)<code>, które mają</code>edge(X, Y)``</p>
<p>– dyrektywa <code>show</code>: bez tego program pokazuje wszystkie atomy wchodzące do rozwiązania (cały stabilny model), co nie jest zawsze potrzebne, a dzięki <code>show</code> program wyświetla tylko <code>degreeOf</code></p>
<p>– <code>/2</code> – liczba argumentów danego predykatu</p>
<p>Wynik:</p>
<pre><code>&gt;clingo degree_count.lp
clingo version 5.4.0
Reading from degree_count.lp

Answer: 1
degreeOf(a, 2) degreeOf(b, 2) degreeOf(c, 2)
</code></pre>
<p>– <code>degree_count.lp</code> – plik tekstowy</p>
<h3 id="przykład-2-sumowanie">Przykład 2: sumowanie</h3>
<pre><code>val(a, 20).
val(b, 12).
val(c, 8).

{in(X)} :- val(X, N). 
:- #sum{N, X : in(X), val(X, N)} != 20. 

#show in/1. //pokaż tylko in z 1. parametrem
</code></pre>
<p>– <code>val(a, 20)</code>, <code>val(b, 12)</code> – fakty: <code>a</code> ma wartość <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mn>20</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">20</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>, <code>b</code> – <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mn>12</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">12</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mord">2</span></span></span></span></span> itd.</p>
<p>– <code>{in(X)} :- val(X, N).</code> – jeśli mamy jakąś wartość przypisaną do <code>X</code>, to albo bierzemy tę wartość do podzbioru, albo ją odrzucamy</p>
<p>– <code>:- #sum{N, X : in(X), val(X, N)} != 20.</code> – więzy: w rozwiązaniu (wśród wybranych <code>in(X)</code>)  nie może być tak, że suma <code>N</code> (w przypadku krotek sumujemy pierwszy element krotki) jest różna od 20 (<code>!= 20</code>)</p>
<p>– czyli sprośród <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span>, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span></span></span></span></span>, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>c</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span></span></span></span></span> wybierz taki podzbiór, których wartości zsumują się do 20</p>
<p>– <code># show in/1.</code> – pokaż tylko wybrane (<code>in</code>)</p>
<p>Wynik</p>
<pre><code>&gt;clingo lata.lp -n 0
clingo version 5.4.0
Reading from lata.lp

Answer: 1
in(b) in(c)
Answer: 2
in(a)
</code></pre>
<h3 id="przykład-3-ekstremum">Przykład 3: ekstremum</h3>
<pre><code>val(a, 20).
val(b, 12).
val(c, 8).

{in(X)} :- val(X, N).
unwantedValue(M) :- M = #min{Y, X : val(X, Y)}. 
:- #sum{N, X: in(X), val(X, N)} != 20. 
:- val(X, N), unwantedValue(N), in(X). 

#show in/1.
</code></pre>
<p>– <code>val(a, 20)</code> itd. – fakty</p>
<p>– <code>{ in(X) } :- val( X, N).</code> – rozwiązanie (<code>in</code>)</p>
<p>– <code>unwantedValue(M) :- M = #min{Y, X : val(X, Y)}.</code> – M to minimum z</p>
<p>– <code>:- #sum{N, X: in(X), val(X, N)} != 20.</code> – jw.</p>
<p>– <code>:- val(X, N), unwantedValue(N), in(X).</code> – nie może być tak, że wybrano <code>X</code>, mające przypisane <code>N</code>, które jest jednocześnie <code>unwantedValue</code></p>
<p>Wynik</p>
<pre><code>Answer: 1
in(a)
</code></pre>
<h3 id="przykład-4-optymalizacja">Przykład 4: optymalizacja</h3>
<pre><code>val(a, 20). 
val(b, 12).
val(c, 8). 

{in(X)} :- val(X, N). 
:- #sum{N, X : in(X), val(X, N)} &gt; 30. 
#maximize{N, X : in(X), val(X, N)}. 

#show in/1.
</code></pre>
<p>– fakty jw.</p>
<p>– <code>{in(X)} :- val(X, N).</code> – jw.</p>
<p>– <code>:- #sum{N, X : in(X), val(X, N)} &gt; 30.</code> – nie może być tak, że suma wybranych elementów jest <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>&gt;</mo><mn>30</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">&gt; 30</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.5782em; vertical-align: -0.0391em;"></span><span class="mrel">&gt;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">3</span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>– <code>#maximize{N, X : in(X), val(X, N)}.</code> – wybierz takie rozwiązanie, które zmaksymalizuje sumę <code>N</code> dodanych do rozwiązania <code>in(X)</code></p>
<p>Wynik:</p>
<pre><code>Answer: 1

Optimizarion: 0
Answer: 2
in(c)
Optimization: -8
[...]
Answer: 5
in(a) in(c)
Optomization: -28
OPTIMUM FOUND
</code></pre>
<p>Jak widać, system maksymalizuje przez minimalizację – wynik maksymalizacji jest z minusem.</p>
<h3 id="przykład-5-maksymalna-klika">Przykład 5: maksymalna klika</h3>
<p>Model:</p>
<pre><code>e(1, 2).
% [...] reszta krawedzi
e(5, 6).
v(X) :- e(X, Y).
v(X) :- e(Y, X).

1 {in(X) : v(X)}.
:- in(X), in(Y), v(X), v(Y), X &lt; Y, not e(X, Y).
#maximize{1, X : in(X)}.

#show in/1.
</code></pre>
<p>– graf zamodelowany zbiorem krawędzi: fakty <code>e(1, 2)</code> itd. oznaczające, że wystęuje krawędź</p>
<p>– generowanie wierzchołków: jeśli coś jest krawędzią (<code>e(X, Y)</code>), to <code>X</code> jest wierzchołkiem (spełnia predykat <code>v</code>)</p>
<p>– bierzemy do rozwiązania minimum 1 wierzchołek: <code>1 {in(X) : v(X)}.</code> (zakładamy, że graf nie jest pusty: ma co najmniej 1 wierzchołek)</p>
<p>– więzy:  wybrane wierzchołki muszą być połączone krawędzią: nie może być tak, że: w rozwiązaniu są 2 różne wierzchołki<code>Y</code> i <code>X</code> zapisane tak, że <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>X</mi><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>Y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">X &lt; Y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.72243em; vertical-align: -0.0391em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&lt;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">Y</span></span></span></span></span> (najpierw mniejszy wierzchołek – a więc graf jest nieskierowany), które nie tworzą krawędzi (predykat <code>e(X, Y)</code> nie jest spełniony)</p>
<p>– maksymalizujemy liczbę wierzchołków w rozwiązaniu (<code>in(X)</code>), w tym celu tworzymy krotki <code>(1, X)</code> z <code>in(X)</code> (sumujemy jedynki)</p>
<p>– <code>show in/1</code> – pokaż same rozwiązania</p>
<h3 id="przykład-6-problem-komiwojażera">Przykład 6: problem komiwojażera</h3>
<p>Fakty</p>
<pre><code>cost(1,2,2). cost(1,3,3). cost(1,4,1).
cost(2,4,2). cost(2,5,2). cost(2,6,4).
cost(3,1,3). cost(3,4,2). cost(3,5,2).
cost(4,1,1). cost(4,2,2).
cost(5,3,2). cost(5,4,2). cost(5,6,1).
cost(6,2,4). cost(6,3,3) cost(6,5,1).
</code></pre>
<p>– ``cost(x, y, z) – x – skąd, y – dokąd, z – ile czasu (jak daleko, koszt przejscia)</p>
<p>– chyba graf skierowany, a więc komiwojazer niesymetryczny (przejście z <code>A</code> do <code>B</code> ma inny koszt niż droga z <code>B</code> do <code>A</code></p>
<p>Model:</p>
<pre><code>edge(X, Y) :- cost(X, Y, _).
node(X) :- cost(X, _, _). 
node(Y): - cost(_, Y, _).

{ cycle(X, Y) : edge(X, Y) } = 1 :- node(X). //jeli wezmiemy cykl, to liczba krawedzi wychodzacych z wierzcholka musi wynosic 1, patrzymy tylko na te wziete do cyklu - krawedz wzieta do cyklu, czyli liczba krawedzi wzietych to cyklu musi byc rowna 1
{ cycle(X, Y) : edge(X, Y) } = 1 :- node(Y). 

reached(Y) :- cycle(1, Y). //ustalamy wierzcholek poczatkowy, jakis numer 1 bedzie, zakladajac, ze numerujemy od 1
reached(Y) :- cycle(X, Y), reached(X). //zeby nie bylo rozlacznych cykli, kiedy Y jest osiagalny z X, jesli do cyklu wzieto X i Y; definijca rekurencyjna
:- node(Y), not reached(Y). //nie moze byc tak, ze jest jakich wiezcholek i on nie jest osiagniety - mowimy, ze kazdy musi byc osiagniety

#minimize{C, X, Y: cycle(X, Y), cost(X, Y, C) }. //przecinek oznacza "i", sumuje C, ale biore pod uwage tylko te, ktore sa w cycle(X, Y) 
</code></pre>
<p>– generowanie krawędzi: <code>edge(X, Y) :- cost(X, Y, _).</code> – niezależnie od kosztu, jeśli para <code>X</code>, <code>Y</code> ma koszt, to jest krawędzią</p>
<p>– graf jest skierowany, bo inaczej model zawierałby regułę mówiącą, że krawędź w jedną stronę jest równa krawędzi w drugą</p>
<p>– generowanie wierzchołków: jeśli istnieje jeden element pary mającej ma koszt (<code>X</code> lub <code>Y</code>), to <code>X</code> (<code>Y</code>) jest wierzchołkiem: to generuj z krawędzi <code>edge</code> cykl (<code>cycle</code>); liczba takich krawędzi wynosi zawsze 1</p>
<p>– ograniczenie (w komiwojażerze graf ma cykl Hamiltona): dla dowolnego wierzchołka <code>X</code> (lub <code>Y</code>)  musi istnieć tylko 1 krawędź wychodząca z tego wierzchołka (stąd jedynka dopisana do każdej krotki)</p>
<p>– ograniczenie: każdy <code>Y</code> wierzchołek, jeśli tworzy cykl z wierzchołkiem startowym (<code>1</code>), to jest osiągalny i jeśli jest osiągalny i jest w cyklu od <code>X</code> do <code>Y</code>, to <code>Y</code> też jest osiągalne</p>
<p>– ograniczeni: wykluczone, że jest jakiś wierzchołek (<code>node(Y)</code>), który nie jest osiągalny: komiwojażer musi odwiedzić wszystkie miejsca</p>
<p>– cel: zminimalizować koszt <code>C</code> generowany na podstawie zbioru krawędzi wziętych do rozwiązania (<code>cycle</code>)</p>
<h3 id="przykład-7-problem-pokrycia">Przykład 7: problem pokrycia</h3>
<p>Definicja pokrycia: dane są:</p>
<ul>
<li>zbiór miast,</li>
<li>czasy przejazdów (możliwe niesymetryczne), między każdą parą miast</li>
<li>dopuszczalny maks. czas <em>max_time</em> dojazdu wozu strażackiego</li>
</ul>
<p>Pytanie: W których miastach rozmieścić remizy strażackie, by nie przekraczając czasu <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>t</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">t</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.61508em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">t</span></span></span></span></span> móc dojechać do każdego miasta i aby liczba wymaganych remiz była najmniejsza?</p>
<p>Fakty</p>
<pre><code>#const num_cities = 6. 			% liczba miast (stala)
#const max_time = 15. 			% maksymalny czas dojazdu (stala)
cities(1 .. num_cities). 		% fakty od 1 do num_cities

% odleglosci miedzy miastami
dist(1, 2, 10). 				% odleglosci 10 miedzy miastami 1 i 2
dist(1, 5, 30).
% [...]
dist(5, 1, 35).
dist(6, 5, 14).

% regula: jesli mamy miasto City, to mamy odleglosc 0 miedzy nim a nim samym
dist(City, City, 0) :- cities(City).

% regula: liczba remiz co najmniej 1
1 { x(City) : cities(City) }. 	% x to predykat - czy miasto City wybrano

% wiezy
:- { x(C2) : cities(C2), dist(C1, C1, Dist), Dist &lt;= max_time } 0, cities(C1).
								% brak cyfry przed lewa klamra - od 0
								% przy ustalonym miescie C1
								% nie moze 0 takich wybranych C2 (x(C2))
